    <a id="13952" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#128" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="13956" class="Number">0</a> <a id="13958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="13960" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#128" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="13964" class="Number">1</a> <a id="13966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="13968" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#128" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="13972" class="Number">2</a> <a id="13974" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="13976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1112" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
  <a id="13981" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#3999" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="13989" class="Number">1</a> <a id="13991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="13993" class="Number">2</a> <a id="13995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="13997" class="Number">3</a> <a id="13999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="14001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1112" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
  <a id="14006" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Map requires time linear in the length of the list.

It is often convenient to exploit currying by applying
map to a function to yield a new function, and at a later
point applying the resulting function.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sucs"></a><a id="14237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#14237" class="Function">sucs</a> <a id="14242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="14249" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="14251" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="14258" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
<a id="14260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#14237" class="Function">sucs</a> <a id="14265" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#13290" class="Function">map</a> <a id="14271" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#128" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a>

  <a id="14384" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#3999" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="14392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="14394" class="Number">1</a> <a id="14396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14398" class="Number">2</a> <a id="14400" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14402" class="Number">3</a> <a id="14404" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="14408" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Any type that is parameterised on another type, such as lists, has a
corresponding map, which accepts a function and returns a function
from the type parameterised on the domain of the function to the type
parameterised on the range of the function. Further, a type that is
parameterised on _n_ types will have a map that is parameterised on
_n_ functions.


#### Exercise `map-compose`

Prove that the map of a composition is equal to the composition of two maps.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14900" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

The last step of the proof requires extensionality.

## Fold {#Fold}

Fold takes an operator and a value, and uses the operator to combine
each of the elements of the list, taking the given value as the result
for the empty list.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="foldr"></a><a id="15871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15877" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15879" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15881" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15882" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15884" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15886" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15888" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="15891" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15893" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15895" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15882" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15898" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15884" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15902" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15884" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15884" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15911" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="15918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15882" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15920" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15884" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="15924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15930" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15934" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1112" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>        <a id="15946" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15934" class="Bound">e</a>
<a id="15951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15957" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15961" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15963" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15964" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="15968" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15968" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="15970" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="15973" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="15976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15964" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15957" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="15980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="15986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15957" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="15990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15961" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="15992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15968" class="Bound">xs</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Fold of the empty list is the given value.
Fold of a non-empty list uses the operator to combine
the head of the list and the fold of the tail of the list.

Here is an example showing how to use fold to find the sum of a list.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16246" class="Function">_</a> <a id="16248" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="16256" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#230" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="16260" class="Number">0</a> <a id="16262" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16264" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16268" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16272" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16276" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="16280" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16282" class="Number">10</a>

  <a id="16552" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Fold requires time linear in the length of the list.

It is often convenient to exploit currying by applying
fold to an operator and a value to yield a new function,
and at a later point applying the resulting function.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sum"></a><a id="16798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16798" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16802" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="16809" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="16811" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16813" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
<a id="16815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16798" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16819" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="16827" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#230" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="16831" class="Number">0</a>

<a id="16834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16834" class="Function">_</a> <a id="16836" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16798" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16842" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16844" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16848" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16852" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16856" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a> <a id="16860" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="16862" class="Number">10</a>
<a id="16865" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="16867" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16871" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#3941" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="16881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#16798" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="16885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16887" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16891" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16895" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16899" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>

    <a id="16913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="16919" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#230" class="Primitive Operator">_+_</a> <a id="16923" class="Number">0</a> <a id="16925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="16927" class="Number">1</a> <a id="16929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16931" class="Number">2</a> <a id="16933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16935" class="Number">3</a> <a id="16937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16939" class="Number">4</a> <a id="16941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="16945" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#3999" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="16953" class="Number">10</a>
  <a id="16958" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4239" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Just as the list type has two constructors, `[]` and `_∷_`,
so the fold function takes two arguments, `e` and `_⊕_`
(in addition to the list argument).
In general, a data type with _n_ constructors will have
a corresponding fold function that takes _n_ arguments.

#### Exercise `product`

Use fold to define a function to find the product of a list of numbers.
For example,

    product [ 1 , 2 , 3 , 4 ] ≡ 24

#### Exercise `foldr-++`

Show that fold and append are related as follows.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17473" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

id="17510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17511" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="17515" class="Symbol">:</a> <a link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17501" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="17523" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17501" class="Bound">B</a><a id="17526" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17529" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17529" #### Exercise `sum-downFrom` (stretch)

Define a function that counts down as follows.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="downFrom"></a><a id="18257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18257" class="Function">downFrom</a> <a id="18266" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18268" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="18270" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="18277" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

For example,
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18376" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18376" class="Function">_</a> <a id="18378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18380" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18257" class="Function">downFrom</a> <a id="18389" class="Number">3</a> <a id="18391" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="18393" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="18395" class="Number">2</a> <a id="18397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18399" class="Number">1</a> <a id="18401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18403" class="Number">0</a> <a id="18405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="18407" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="18409" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18411" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Monoids

Typically when we use a fold the operator is associative and the
value is a left and right identity for the value, meaning that the
operator and the value form a _monoid_.

We can define a monoid as a suitable record type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18862" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="IsMonoid"></a><a id="18869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18869" class="Record">IsMonoid</a> <a id="18878" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18879" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18881" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18883" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="18886" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18888" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18889" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="18893" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18897" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18901" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18903" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18904" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18907" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="18909" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a><a id="18912" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18914" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18916" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="18920" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="18928" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="IsMonoid.assoc"></a><a id="18938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18938" class="Field">assoc</a> <a id="18944" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18946"     <a id="IsMonoid.identityˡ"></a><a id="18992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18992" class="Field">identityˡ</a> <a id="19002" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19004" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19006" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19007" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19009" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19012" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19014" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18907" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="19018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18889" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="19020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19007" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19022" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="19024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19007" class="Bound">x</a>
    <a id="IsMonoid.identityʳ"></a><a id="19030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19030" class="Field">identityʳ</a> <a id="19040" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19042" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19044" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19047" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18879" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19050" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19052" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19045" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="19056" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18889" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="19058" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18907" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="19060" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="19062" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#19045" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="19065" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18869" class="Module">IsMonoid</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As examples, sum and zero, multiplication and one, and append and the empty
list, are all examples of monoids.

If `_⊕_` and `e` form a monoid, then we can re-express fold on the
same operator and an arbitrary value.

## All {#All}

We can also define predicates over lists. Two of the most important
are `All` and `Any`.

Predicate `All P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by every element of a list.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21064" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="All"></a><a id="21069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21073" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21074" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21076" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21078" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="21081" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21083" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21084" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21086" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21074" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21090" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21092" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="21095" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21097" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="21104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21074" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21106" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21108" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="21112" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="All.[]"></a><a id="21120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21120" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="21123" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21084" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21131" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1112" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
  <a id="All._∷_"></a><a id="21136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_∷_</a> <a id="21140" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21142" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21143" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21074" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21148" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21150" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21151" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="21154" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="21161" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21074" class="Bound">A</a><a id="21162" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="21164" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21084" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21143" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21170" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21084" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21151" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="21181" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21084" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="21189" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21143" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="21192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="21194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21151" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="21196" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
The type has two constructors, reusing the names of the same constructors for lists.
The first asserts that `P` holds for ever element of the empty list.
The second asserts that if `P` holds of the head of a list and for every
element of the tail of a list, then `P` holds for every element of the list.
Agda uses types to disambiguate whether the constructor is building
a list or evidence that `All P` holds.

For example, `All (_≤ 2)` holds of a list where every element is less
than or equal to two.  Recall that `z≤n` proves `zero ≤ n` for any
`n`, and that if `m≤n` proves `m ≤ n` then `s≤s m≤n` proves `suc m ≤
suc n`, for any `m` and `n`.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21869" class="Function">_</a> <a id="21871" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="21877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21878" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#742" class="Datatype Operator">_≤</a> <a id="21881" class="Number">2</a><a id="21882" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="21886" class="Number">0</a> <a id="21888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21890" class="Number">1</a> <a id="21892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="21894" class="Number">2</a> <a id="21896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2960" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="21898" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="21900" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="21902" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#765" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a> <a id="21906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="21908" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21909" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#807" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="21913" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#765" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a><a id="21916" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="21918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="21920" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21921" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#807" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="21925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21926" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#807" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="21930" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Nat.Base.html#765" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a><a id="21933" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="21936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="21938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21120" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Here `_∷_` and `[]` are the constructors of `All P` rather than of `List A`.
The three items are proofs of `0 ≤ 2`, `1 ≤ 2`, and `2 ≤ 2`, respectively.

## Any

Predicate `Any P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by some element of a list.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22207" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Any"></a><a id="22212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22216" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22217" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22219" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22221" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="22224" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22226" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="22229" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22233" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22235" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="22238" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="22247" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22249" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22251" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="22255" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Any.here"></a><a id="22263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22263" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="22268" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="22271" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22272" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22277" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22279" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22280" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22283" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="22290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22293" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="22297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22272" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22299" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22301" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="22307" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22272" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="22312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22280" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="22314" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="Any.there"></a><a id="22318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22318" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="22324" class="Symbol">:</a> <a %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22335" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22340" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="22345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22217" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22346" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22348" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22350" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="22356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22335" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22359" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22227" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="22367" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22327" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="22372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22335" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="22374" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
The first constructor provides evidence that the head of the list
satisfies `P`, while the second provides evidence that some element of
the tail of the list satisfies `P`.  For example, we can define list
membership as follows.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22629" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="22635" class="Number">4</a> <a id="22637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a>

<a id="_∈_"></a><a id="22642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="22646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22648" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22650" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22653" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22655" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="22658" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22661" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22663" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22666" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22668" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22669" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="22679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22651" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22680" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22682" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22684" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="22688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22688" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="22692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22692" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22695" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="22701" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22688" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22704" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡_</a><a id="22706" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22692" class="Bound">xs</a>

<a id="_∉_"></a><a id="22712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22712" class="Function Operator">_∉_</a> <a id="22716" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22718" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22720" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22721" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22721" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22723" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22725" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="22728" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22730" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22731" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22733" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22735" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22721" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22736" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22739" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="22749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22721" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22750" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22752" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22754" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="22758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22758" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22712" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="22762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22762" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="22765" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22767" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="22769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22758" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="22772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="22774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22762" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="22776" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
For example, zero is an element of the list `[ 0 , 1 , 0 , 2 ]`.  Indeed, we can demonstrate
this fact in two different ways, corresponding to the two different
occurrences of zero in the list, as the first element and as the third element.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23043" class="Function">_</a> <a id="23045" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23047" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="23053" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23057" class="Number">1</a> <a id="23059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23061" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23065" class="Number">2</a> <a id="23067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="23069" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="23071" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22263" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="23078" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

<a id="23084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23084" class="Function">_</a> <a id="23086" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23088" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23090" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22642" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="23092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="23094" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23098" class="Number">1</a> <a id="23100" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23102" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23104" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23106" class="Number">2</a> <a id="23108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="23110" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="23112" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22318" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="23120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22318" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="23127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22263" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="23133" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="23137" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Further, we can demonstrate that three is not in the list, because
any possible proof that it is in the list leads to contradiction.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-in"></a><a id="23297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#23297" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="23304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23306" class="Number">3</a> <a id="23308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22712" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="23310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="23312" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23316" class="Number">1</a> <a id="23318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23320" class="Number">0</a> <a id="23322" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23324" class="Number">2</a> <a id="23326" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#2999" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>

The five occurrences of `()` attest to the fact that there is no
possible evidence for `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 1`, `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 2`, and
`3 ∈ []`, respectively.

## All and append

A predicate holds for every element of one list appended to another if and
only if it holds for every element of each list.  Indeed, an even stronger
result is true, as we can show that the two types are isomorphic.

Operator">⟩</a> <a id="25035" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25037" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

#### Exercise `Any-++`

Prove a result similar to `All-++`, but with `Any` in place of `All`, and a suitable
replacement for `_×_`.  As a consequence, demonstrate an isomorphism relating
`_∈_` and `_++_`.

#### Exercise `¬Any≃All¬` (stretch)

First generalise composition to arbitrary levels, using
[universe polymorphism]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Equality.md%}#unipoly).
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘′_"></a><a id="25414" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25414" class="Function Operator">_∘′_</a> <a id="25419" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25421" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25423" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25424" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a> <a id="25427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25427" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a> <a id="25430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25430" class="Bound">ℓ₃</a> <a id="25433" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25435" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="25440" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25442" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25443" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25445" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25447" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="25451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25424" class="Bound">ℓ₁</a><a id="25453" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25456" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25460" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="25464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25427" class="Bound">ℓ₂</a><a id="25466" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25468" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25469" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="25471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25473" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="25477" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25430" class="Bound">ℓ₃</a><a id="25479" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="25483" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25456" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25469" class="Bound">C</a><a id="25491" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25493" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25495" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25443" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25498" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25456" class="Bound">B</a><a id="25501" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25503" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25443" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25507" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25469" class="Bound">C</a>
<a id="25511" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25512" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25512" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="25514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25414" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="25517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25517" class="Bound">f</a><a id="25518" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25520" class="Bound">x</a>  <a id="25523" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="25526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25512" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="25528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25529" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25517" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="25531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25520" class="Bound">x</a><a id="25532" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Show that `Any` and `All` satisfy a version of De Morgan's Law.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25623" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

    <a id="25691" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25693" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25694" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬_</a> <a id="25697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25414" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="25700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#22212" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="25704" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25660" class="Bound">P</a><a id="25705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25674" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="25710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Record Operator">≃</a> <a id="25712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="25716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25717" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬_</a> <a id="25720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25414" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="25723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25660" class="Bound">P</a><a id="25724" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25674" class="Bound">xs</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Do we also have the following?

If so, prove; if not, explain why.


## Decidability of All

If we consider a predicate as a function that yields a boolean,
it is easy to define an analogue of `All`, which returns true if
a given predicate returns true for every element of a list.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="all"></a><a id="26165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26165" class="Function">all</a> <a id="26169" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26171" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26173" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26174" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26176" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26178" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26181" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26183" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26185" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26174" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26188" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26190" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#67" class="Datatype">Bool</a><a id="26194" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26196" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1083" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="26203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26174" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26205" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26207" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#67" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="26212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26165" class="Function">all</a> <a id="26216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26216" class="Bound">p</a>  <a id="26219" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="26222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#15871" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="26228" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Bool.Base.html#1012" class="Function Operator">_∧_</a> <a id="26232" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#92" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a> <a id="26237" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="26239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#13290" class="Function">map</a> <a id="26243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26216" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
The function can be written in a particularly compact style by
using the higher-order functions `map` and `foldr`.

As one would hope, if we replace booleans by decidables there is again
an analogue of `All`.  First, return to the notion of a predicate `P` as
a function of type `A → Set`, taking a value `x` of type `A` into evidence
`P x` that a property holds for `x`.  Say that a predicate `P` is _decidable_
if we have a function that for a given `x` can decide `P x`.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Decidable"></a><a id="26743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26743" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="26753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26755" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26757" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26758" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26760" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26762" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26765" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26767" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26758" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26772" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26774" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26777" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26779" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26781" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="26785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26743" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="26795" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26796" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26797" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26799" class="Bound">P</a>  <a id="26802" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="26805" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26808" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="26810" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26796" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26813" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26815" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26817" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="26821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26799" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="26824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26808" class="Bound">x</a><a id="26825" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Then if predicate `P` is decidable, it is also decidable whether every
element of a list satisfies the predicate.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="All?"></a><a id="26965" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26965" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="26970" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26972" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26974" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26975" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26977" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26979" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26982" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26984" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26985" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="26987" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26975" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="26991" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26993" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="26996" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26998" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26743" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26985" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="27012" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26743" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="27024" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21069" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="27029" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26985" class="Bound">P</a><a id="27030" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26965" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27037" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1112" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>                                 <a id="27075" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27078" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27082" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21120" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
<a id="27085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26965" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27090" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27090" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27093" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27094" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="27096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1127" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27098" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="27100" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27102" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="27107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27090" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27094" class="Bound">x</a>   <a id="27114" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#26965" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="27121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27090" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="27124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27098" class="Bound">xs</a>
<a id="27127" class="Symbol">...</a>                 <a id="27147" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27149" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27153" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27156" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27158" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27162" class="Bound">Pxs</a>     <a id="27170" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27173" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="27177" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27153" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27162" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27186" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="27188" class="Symbol">...</a>                 <a id="27208" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27210" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27213" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="27217" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="27219" class="Symbol">_</a>           <a id="27231" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27234" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27237" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="27240" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27241" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27246" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27249" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27251" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27213" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="27257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27241" class="Bound">Px</a>   <a id="27262" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="27264" class="CatchallClause Symbol">...</a><a id="27267" class="CatchallClause">                 </a><a id="27284" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="27285" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27286" class="CatchallClause Symbol">_</a><a id="27287" class="CatchallClause">      </a><a id="27293" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="27294" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27295" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="CatchallClause InductiveConstructor">no</a><a id="27297" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="27298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27298" class="CatchallClause Bound">¬Pxs</a>     <a id="27307" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="27310" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="27313" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="27316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27317" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="27320" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21136" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="27322" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27322" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="27325" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="27327" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="27329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27298" class="Bound">¬Pxs</a> <a id="27334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#27322" class="Bound">Pxs</a> <a id="27338" class="Symbol">}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
If the list is empty, then trivially `P` holds for every element of
the list.  Otherwise, the structure of the proof is similar to that
showing that the conjuction of two decidable propositions is itself
decidable, using `_∷_` rather than `⟨_,_⟩` to combine the evidence for
the head and tail of the list.

#### Exercise `any?`

Just as `All` has analogues `all` and `all?` which determine whether a
predicate holds for every element of a list, so does `Any` have
analogues `any` and `any?` which determine whether a predicates holds
for some element of a list.  Give their definitions.


## Standard Library

Definitions similar to those in this chapter can be found in the standard library.

The standard library version of `IsMonoid` differs from the
one given here, in that it is also parameterised on an equivalence relation.


## Unicode

This chapter uses the following unicode.

    ∷  U+2237  PROPORTION  (\::)
    ⊗  U+2297  CIRCLED TIMES  (\otimes)
    ∈  U+2208  ELEMENT OF  (\in)
    ∉  U+2209  NOT AN ELEMENT OF  (\inn)
